    <h2>Important: Please Read Before Proceeding</h2>

    <p>This tool is provided for <strong>educational and informational purposes only</strong>. It is designed to help you understand your kidney function results — not to replace medical advice, diagnosis, or treatment.</p>

    <p>Calculations are based on published clinical guidelines (NICE NG203, CKD-EPI 2021, KFRE). However, <strong>individual circumstances vary greatly</strong> — guidelines should never be applied rigidly.</p>

    <p><strong>If you feel unwell, have concerning symptoms, or are unsure about any result — contact your GP or NHS 111 promptly.</strong> In an emergency, call 999.</p>

    <p>Developed by Dr Christopher Lawrence, Consultant Nephrologist. Not a substitute for a consultation with your own doctor.</p>

  </div>

  <div id="fr-advice" class="hidden" style="margin-top:18px">

    <div class="ib blue"><strong>Important note about single readings:</strong> The eGFR is not validated where kidney function may be rapidly changing, and one-off 'sinker' results are well recognised — a single low reading may not reflect your true baseline. A confirmatory test is recommended before any diagnosis is made.</div>

    <div id="retest-box"></div>

  </div>

    </div>

The eGFR values shown in the chart are all calculated using the CKD-EPI 2021 equation and may therefore differ slightly from the eGFR values you were given at the time.</div>

<div class="card hidden fi" id="c-acr">

  <div class="card-hdr">

    <div class="c-icon">🧪</div>

    <div><div class="c-title">Urine Albumin:Creatinine Ratio (ACR)</div><div class="c-sub">Detects protein in the urine — a key marker of kidney damage</div></div>

  </div>

  <div class="rgrp">

    <label class="ropt"><input type="radio" name="acr" value="no" onchange="handleACR(this)"><div class="ot"><strong>I haven't had a urine ACR done</strong><span>Or I'm not sure</span></div></label>

    <label class="ropt"><input type="radio" name="acr" value="yes" onchange="handleACR(this)"><div class="ot"><strong>Yes — I have an ACR result to enter</strong><span>I'd like to see my full CKD risk category</span></div></label>

  </div>

  <div id="acr-no" class="hidden" style="margin-top:14px">

    <div class="ib blue"><strong>Recommended next step:</strong> Ask your GP or practice nurse for a urine ACR test. This is a simple urine sample (ideally your first morning sample) that checks for protein — a key marker of kidney damage not captured by eGFR alone. It is essential for accurately staging CKD and estimating progression risk.</div>

  </div>

  <div id="acr-yes" class="hidden" style="margin-top:14px">

    <div class="fgrp" style="max-width:320px">

  <div class="card-hdr">

    <div class="c-icon">💊</div>

    <div><div class="c-title">Blood Pressure</div><div class="c-sub">BP control is one of the most important factors in slowing CKD</div></div>

  </div>

  <div class="rgrp">

    <label class="ropt"><input type="radio" name="bp" value="no" onchange="handleBP(this)"><div class="ot"><strong>I don't know my blood pressure</strong><span>I haven't had it checked recently</span></div></label>

    <label class="ropt"><input type="radio" name="bp" value="yes" onchange="handleBP(this)"><div class="ot"><strong>I know my blood pressure reading</strong><span>I'd like to enter it</span></div></label>

  </div>

  <div id="bp-no" class="hidden" style="margin-top:14px">

    <div class="ib blue"><strong>How to check your blood pressure:</strong> You can get it checked at your GP surgery, a pharmacy (many offer free checks), or using a home blood pressure monitor (~£25–£40 from pharmacies and online). Friends or family with a monitor may also be able to help. Regular home monitoring is often more accurate than a single clinic reading.</div>

  </div>

  <div class="nicebox">

    <strong>About these recommendations:</strong> This tool references <strong>NICE CKD Guidelines (NG203)</strong> and uses the internationally validated CKD-EPI 2021, Cockcroft–Gault, and KFRE equations. Guidelines are a framework — not a rigid rulebook. Every patient's situation is individual. Use this as a starting point for a conversation with your GP, and ask about a referral to a nephrologist if you have concerns. <em>Do not act on these results alone.</em>

<script>

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────

// STATE

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────

let useMgDL = false;

let useACRmgg = false;

let useImperialHeight = false;

let useImperialWeight = false;

let curEGFR = null, curAge = null, curSex = null;

let curACR_mgmmol = null;

let prevReadings = [];

let chartInst = null;


// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────

// LOCAL STORAGE — persist & restore

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────

const LS_KEY = 'kidneyChecker_v1';


function saveToStorage() {

  try {

    const data = {

      inputs: {

        age: document.getElementById('age').value,

        sex: document.querySelector('input[name="sex"]:checked')?.value,

        height: document.getElementById('height').value,

        htFt: document.getElementById('htFt').value,

        htIn: document.getElementById('htIn').value,

        weight: document.getElementById('weight').value,

        wtSt: document.getElementById('wtSt').value,

        wtLbs: document.getElementById('wtLbs').value,

        creat: document.getElementById('creat').value,

        rDate: document.getElementById('rDate').value,

        name: document.getElementById('patientName').value,

        useMgDL, useImperialHeight, useImperialWeight,

        creatToggle: document.getElementById('creatToggle').checked,

        htToggle: document.getElementById('htToggle').checked,

        wtToggle: document.getElementById('wtToggle').checked,

      },

      prevReadings,

      curEGFR, curAge, curSex, curACR_mgmmol,

    };

    localStorage.setItem(LS_KEY, JSON.stringify(data));

  } catch(e) {}

}


function loadFromStorage() {

  try {

    const raw = localStorage.getItem(LS_KEY);

    if (!raw) return false;

    const data = JSON.parse(raw);

    const inp = data.inputs || {};


    if (inp.name) document.getElementById('patientName').value = inp.name;

    if (inp.age) document.getElementById('age').value = inp.age;

    if (inp.sex) {

      document.querySelectorAll('input[name="sex"]').forEach(r => r.checked = r.value === inp.sex);

    }

    if (inp.useMgDL) { document.getElementById('creatToggle').checked = true; toggleCreat(); }

    if (inp.creat) document.getElementById('creat').value = inp.creat;

    if (inp.rDate) document.getElementById('rDate').value = inp.rDate;


    if (inp.useImperialHeight) {

      document.getElementById('htToggle').checked = true; toggleHeight();

      if (inp.htFt) document.getElementById('htFt').value = inp.htFt;

      if (inp.htIn) document.getElementById('htIn').value = inp.htIn;

    } else {

      if (inp.height) document.getElementById('height').value = inp.height;

    }


    if (inp.useImperialWeight) {

      document.getElementById('wtToggle').checked = true; toggleWeight();

      if (inp.wtSt) document.getElementById('wtSt').value = inp.wtSt;

      if (inp.wtLbs) document.getElementById('wtLbs').value = inp.wtLbs;

    } else {

      if (inp.weight) document.getElementById('weight').value = inp.weight;

    }


    prevReadings = data.prevReadings || [];

    curEGFR = data.curEGFR;

    curAge = data.curAge;

    curSex = data.curSex;

    curACR_mgmmol = data.curACR_mgmmol;


    if (curEGFR) {

      // Re-run calculate to restore results

      calculate(true);

    }

    return true;

  } catch(e) { return false; }

}


function resetData() {

  if (!confirm('Clear all saved data and start over?')) return;

  localStorage.removeItem(LS_KEY);

  location.reload();

}


// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────

// HEIGHT TOGGLE — cm ↔ ft & in

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────

function toggleHeight() {

  useImperialHeight = document.getElementById('htToggle').checked;

  const cmWrap = document.getElementById('ht-cm-wrap');

  const impWrap = document.getElementById('ht-imp-wrap');

  const lbl = document.getElementById('htUnitLbl');

  const tog = document.getElementById('htTogTxt');

  if (useImperialHeight) {

    cmWrap.classList.add('hidden');

    impWrap.classList.remove('hidden');

    lbl.textContent = 'ft & in';

    tog.textContent = 'cm';

  } else {

    cmWrap.classList.remove('hidden');

    impWrap.classList.add('hidden');

    lbl.textContent = 'cm';

    tog.textContent = 'ft & in';

  }

  liveRecalc();

}


function getHeightCm() {

  if (useImperialHeight) {

    const ft = parseFloat(document.getElementById('htFt').value) || 0;

    const inches = parseFloat(document.getElementById('htIn').value) || 0;

    return (ft * 12 + inches) * 2.54;

  }

  return parseFloat(document.getElementById('height').value);

}


// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────

// WEIGHT TOGGLE — kg ↔ stones & lbs

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────

function toggleWeight() {

  useImperialWeight = document.getElementById('wtToggle').checked;

  const kgWrap = document.getElementById('wt-kg-wrap');

  const impWrap = document.getElementById('wt-imp-wrap');

  const lbl = document.getElementById('wtUnitLbl');

  const tog = document.getElementById('wtTogTxt');

  if (useImperialWeight) {

    kgWrap.classList.add('hidden');

    impWrap.classList.remove('hidden');

    lbl.textContent = 'st & lbs';

    tog.textContent = 'kg';

  } else {

    kgWrap.classList.remove('hidden');

    impWrap.classList.add('hidden');

    lbl.textContent = 'kg';

    tog.textContent = 'st & lbs';

  }

  liveRecalc();

}


function getWeightKg() {

  if (useImperialWeight) {

    const st = parseFloat(document.getElementById('wtSt').value) || 0;

    const lbs = parseFloat(document.getElementById('wtLbs').value) || 0;

    return (st * 14 + lbs) * 0.453592;

  }

  return parseFloat(document.getElementById('weight').value);

}


// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────

// CREATININE UNIT TOGGLE

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────

function toggleCreat() {

  useMgDL = document.getElementById('creatToggle').checked;

  if (useMgDL) {

    document.getElementById('creatTogLbl').textContent = 'switch to μmol/L';

    document.getElementById('creatLbl').textContent = 'Serum Creatinine (mg/dL)';

    document.getElementById('creatU').textContent = 'mg/dL';

    document.getElementById('prevCU').textContent = 'mg/dL';

    document.getElementById('creat').placeholder = 'e.g. 1.2';

    document.getElementById('prev-creat').placeholder = 'Creatinine mg/dL';

  } else {

    document.getElementById('creatTogLbl').textContent = 'switch to mg/dL';

    document.getElementById('creatLbl').textContent = 'Serum Creatinine (μmol/L)';

    document.getElementById('creatU').textContent = 'μmol/L';

    document.getElementById('prevCU').textContent = 'μmol/L';

    document.getElementById('creat').placeholder = 'e.g. 110';

    document.getElementById('prev-creat').placeholder = 'Creatinine';

  }

  liveRecalc();

}


// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────

// ACR UNIT TOGGLE  mg/mmol (UK) ↔ mg/g (US)

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────

function toggleACR() {

  useACRmgg = document.getElementById('acrToggle').checked;

  if (useACRmgg) {

    document.getElementById('acrTogLbl').textContent = 'switch to mg/mmol';

    document.getElementById('acrU').textContent = 'mg/g';

    document.getElementById('acrLbl').textContent = 'ACR result (mg/g) — US standard';

  } else {

    document.getElementById('acrTogLbl').textContent = 'switch to mg/g';

    document.getElementById('acrU').textContent = 'mg/mmol';

    document.getElementById('acrLbl').textContent = 'ACR result (mg/mmol) — UK standard';

  }

  const v = parseFloat(document.getElementById('acr-in').value);

  if (v) showACR();

}


// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────

// CKD-EPI 2021 (race-free)

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────

function calcEGFR(age, sex, scrMgDL) {

  const female = sex === 'female';

  const kappa = female ? 0.7 : 0.9;

  const alpha = female ? -0.241 : -0.302;

  const r = scrMgDL / kappa;

  let e = 142 * Math.pow(Math.min(r,1), alpha) * Math.pow(Math.max(r,1), -1.200) * Math.pow(0.9938, age);

  if (female) e *= 1.012;

  return Math.round(e * 10) / 10;

}


function stageOf(egfr) {

  if (egfr >= 90) return {stage:'G1', desc:'Normal or high kidney function', cls:'g1', idx:0};

  if (egfr >= 60) return {stage:'G2', desc:'Mildly decreased kidney function', cls:'g2', idx:1};

  if (egfr >= 45) return {stage:'G3a', desc:'Mildly to moderately decreased', cls:'g3a', idx:2};

  if (egfr >= 30) return {stage:'G3b', desc:'Moderately to severely decreased', cls:'g3b', idx:3};

  if (egfr >= 15) return {stage:'G4', desc:'Severely decreased kidney function', cls:'g4', idx:4};

  return {stage:'G5', desc:'Kidney failure range', cls:'g5', idx:5};

}


function acrCatOf(mgmmol) {

  if (mgmmol < 3) return 0;

  if (mgmmol < 30) return 1;

  return 2;

}


// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────

// BMI & COCKCROFT-GAULT

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────

function ibwOf(sex, htCm) { const h = htCm - 152.4; return sex === 'male' ? 50 + 0.906*h : 45.5 + 0.906*h; }

function calcCG(age, sex, scrMgDL, wt, ht) {

  const ibw = ibwOf(sex, ht);

  const bwU = wt > ibw ? ibw + 0.4*(wt - ibw) : wt;

  let cg = ((140 - age) * bwU) / (72 * scrMgDL);

  if (sex === 'female') cg *= 0.85;

  return { cg: Math.round(cg*10)/10, ibw: ibw.toFixed(1), bwU: bwU.toFixed(1) };

}


// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────

// CALCULATE

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────

function calculate(silent) {

  const age = parseFloat(document.getElementById('age').value);

  const sex = document.querySelector('input[name="sex"]:checked').value;

  const ht  = getHeightCm();

  const wt  = getWeightKg();

  const creatRaw = parseFloat(document.getElementById('creat').value);


  if (!silent && (!age || !ht || !wt || !creatRaw)) { alert('Please fill in all fields.'); return; }

  if (!age || !ht || !wt || !creatRaw) return;


  const scrMgDL = useMgDL ? creatRaw : creatRaw / 88.42;

  curAge = age; curSex = sex;

  curEGFR = calcEGFR(age, sex, scrMgDL);


  const si = stageOf(curEGFR);

  const banner = document.getElementById('egfr-banner');

  document.getElementById('egfr-val').textContent = curEGFR;

  banner.className = 'rbanner ' + si.cls;

  // Brief flash to confirm live update

  banner.classList.remove('live-flash');

  void banner.offsetWidth; // force reflow

  banner.classList.add('live-flash');

  document.getElementById('ckd-stage').textContent = 'CKD Stage ' + si.stage;


  const bmi = wt / ((ht/100)**2);

  const bmiOut = bmi < 20 || bmi > 25;

  document.getElementById('bmi-val').textContent = bmi.toFixed(1);

  const bf = document.getElementById('bmi-flag');

  if (bmi < 18.5)     { bf.textContent = '⚠ Underweight (< 18.5)';  bf.style.color = 'var(--orange)'; }

  else if (bmi < 20)  { bf.textContent = '⚠ Low-normal (< 20)';     bf.style.color = 'var(--yellow)'; }

  else if (bmi <= 25) { bf.textContent = '✓ Healthy BMI (20–25)';    bf.style.color = 'var(--green)'; }

  else if (bmi <= 30) { bf.textContent = '⚠ Overweight (25–30)';     bf.style.color = 'var(--yellow)'; }

  else                { bf.textContent = '⚠ Obese (> 30)';            bf.style.color = 'var(--orange)'; }


  const cgSec = document.getElementById('cg-section');

  if (bmiOut) {

    cgSec.classList.remove('hidden');

    const { cg, ibw, bwU } = calcCG(age, sex, scrMgDL, wt, ht);

    document.getElementById('cg-val').textContent = cg;

    document.getElementById('cg-note').textContent =

      `Ideal body weight: ${ibw} kg → Adjusted body weight: ${bwU} kg. ` +

      (bmi < 20 ? 'Low muscle mass in lean patients can make creatinine-based estimates unreliable.'

                : 'In obesity, adjusted BW avoids overestimating creatinine clearance.');

  } else { cgSec.classList.add('hidden'); }


  renderAdvice(curEGFR);

  renderFullStage(curEGFR, curACR_mgmmol);


  ['c-results','c-trend','c-acr','c-bp','c-report','c-res'].forEach(id =>

    document.getElementById(id).classList.remove('hidden'));


  if (!silent) {

    saveToStorage();

    setTimeout(() => document.getElementById('c-results').scrollIntoView({behavior:'smooth',block:'start'}), 100);

  }


  // Restore chart if prevReadings exist

  if (prevReadings.length > 0) {

    renderList();

    renderChart();

  }

}


function renderFullStage(egfr, acrMgMmol) {

  const el = document.getElementById('ckd-full-stage');

  if (!el) return;

  if (!egfr) { el.innerHTML = ''; return; }

  const si = stageOf(egfr);

  let acrLabel = '';

  let acrDesc = '';

  if (acrMgMmol !== null) {

    if (acrMgMmol < 3)       { acrLabel = ' A1'; acrDesc = 'No significant albuminuria'; }

    else if (acrMgMmol < 30) { acrLabel = ' A2'; acrDesc = 'Moderately increased albuminuria'; }

    else                      { acrLabel = ' A3'; acrDesc = 'Severely increased albuminuria'; }

  }

  // Combined: eGFR description · ACR description (no duplication of stage number)

  const parts = [si.desc];

  if (acrDesc) parts.push(acrDesc);

  else parts.push('Enter ACR below for full classification');

  el.innerHTML = parts.join(' &nbsp;·&nbsp; ');

  // Update the stage label to include ACR category

  const stageEl = document.getElementById('ckd-stage');

  if (stageEl) stageEl.textContent = 'CKD Stage ' + si.stage + acrLabel;

}


function renderAdvice(egfr) {

  const b = document.getElementById('advice-boxes');

  if (egfr >= 90) b.innerHTML = `<div class="ib green"><strong>eGFR ≥ 90 (G1):</strong> Your eGFR is in the normal range. However, eGFR alone doesn't tell the whole story — kidney disease can exist with a normal eGFR if there is protein in the urine. Please work through the steps below.</div>`;

  else if (egfr >= 60) b.innerHTML = `<div class="ib green"><strong>eGFR 60–89 (G2):</strong> Mildly reduced — this may be normal for your age. Monitoring is important. Please work through the steps below to get the full picture.</div>`;

  else if (egfr >= 45) b.innerHTML = `<div class="ib yellow"><strong>eGFR 45–59 (G3a):</strong> Moderately reduced. A confirmatory repeat blood test is recommended within <strong>8 weeks</strong>. <em>⚠ If you feel unwell at any point, contact your GP or NHS 111 promptly — don't wait.</em></div>`;

  else if (egfr >= 30) b.innerHTML = `<div class="ib yellow"><strong>eGFR 30–44 (G3b):</strong> Moderately to severely reduced. Repeat blood tests within <strong>4 weeks</strong>. Discuss with your GP and ask about nephrology referral. <em>⚠ If unwell: contact your GP or NHS 111 the same day.</em></div>`;

  else if (egfr >= 15) b.innerHTML = `<div class="ib orange"><strong>eGFR 15–29 (G4):</strong> Severely reduced. Contact your GP <strong>as soon as possible</strong>. This warrants urgent review and likely nephrology referral. <strong>If unwell: call NHS 111 or go to A&amp;E.</strong></div>`;

  else b.innerHTML = `<div class="ib red"><strong>eGFR &lt; 15 (G5):</strong> Kidney failure range. <strong>Please seek medical attention urgently.</strong> Contact your GP today, call NHS 111, or attend A&amp;E if you feel unwell. Do not wait.</div>`;

}


// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────

// FIRST / PREVIOUS READINGS

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────

function handleFR(r) {

  document.getElementById('fr-advice').classList.add('hidden');

  document.getElementById('multi-readings').classList.add('hidden');

  if (r.value === 'yes') {

    document.getElementById('fr-advice').classList.remove('hidden');

    renderRetest(curEGFR);

  } else {

    document.getElementById('multi-readings').classList.remove('hidden');

    renderList(); renderChart();

  }

  saveToStorage();

}


function renderRetest(egfr) {

  const b = document.getElementById('retest-box');

  if (!egfr) { b.innerHTML=''; return; }

  let t, c;

  if (egfr >= 60) { t = '8 weeks'; c = 'green'; }

  else if (egfr >= 30) { t = '4 weeks'; c = 'yellow'; }

  else { t = 'as soon as possible — contact your GP urgently'; c = 'orange'; }

  b.innerHTML = `<div class="ib ${c}" style="margin-top:12px"><strong>Recommended:</strong> Repeat blood tests within <strong>${t}</strong>.<br><br>A single eGFR can be misleading — illness, dehydration, strenuous exercise or certain medications can all temporarily lower the result. A confirmatory test is needed before any diagnosis is made.<br><br><em>⚠ If you feel unwell at any point, don't wait — contact your GP or call NHS 111.</em></div>`;

}


// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────

// READINGS (creatinine-based)

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────

function fmtDate(d) {

  if (!d) return '';

  const [y,m,day] = d.split('-');

  const mn = ['Jan','Feb','Mar','Apr','May','Jun','Jul','Aug','Sep','Oct','Nov','Dec'];

  return `${parseInt(day)} ${mn[parseInt(m)-1]} ${y}`;

}

function creatDisp(mgdl) {

  return useMgDL ? mgdl.toFixed(2) + ' mg/dL' : Math.round(mgdl*88.42) + ' μmol/L';

}

function addReading() {

  const date = document.getElementById('prev-date').value;

  const cr = parseFloat(document.getElementById('prev-creat').value);

  if (!date || !cr) { alert('Please enter a date and creatinine value.'); return; }

  const scrMgDL = useMgDL ? cr : cr / 88.42;

  const egfr = calcEGFR(curAge, curSex, scrMgDL);

  prevReadings = prevReadings.filter(r => r.date !== date);

  prevReadings.push({ date, creat_mgdl: scrMgDL, egfr });

  prevReadings.sort((a,b) => a.date.localeCompare(b.date));

  document.getElementById('prev-date').value = '';

  document.getElementById('prev-creat').value = '';

  renderList(); renderChart();

  saveToStorage();

}

function removeReading(d) {

  prevReadings = prevReadings.filter(r => r.date !== d);

  renderList(); renderChart();

  saveToStorage();

}

function renderList() {

  const list = document.getElementById('r-list');

  let all = [...prevReadings];

  const cd = document.getElementById('rDate').value;

  const crRaw = parseFloat(document.getElementById('creat').value);

  if (cd && crRaw && curEGFR) {

    const scrMgDL = useMgDL ? crRaw : crRaw / 88.42;

    if (!all.find(r => r.date === cd)) {

      all.push({ date: cd, creat_mgdl: scrMgDL, egfr: curEGFR, cur: true });

      all.sort((a,b) => a.date.localeCompare(b.date));

    }

  }

  if (!all.length) { list.innerHTML='<div style="color:var(--text-muted);font-size:13px">No readings added yet.</div>'; return; }

  list.innerHTML = all.map(r => `

    <div class="r-item">

      <span class="r-date">${fmtDate(r.date)}</span>

      <span style="font-size:13px;color:var(--text-muted)">${creatDisp(r.creat_mgdl)}</span>

      <span class="r-val">${r.egfr} <small style="font-weight:400;color:var(--text-muted)">mL/min</small></span>

      ${r.cur

        ? '<span style="font-size:11px;color:var(--accent);font-weight:500;white-space:nowrap">Current</span>'

        : `<button class="r-del" onclick="removeReading('${r.date}')">✕</button>`}

    </div>`).join('');

}


// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────

// CHART — time-proportionate x-axis using real dates

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────

function dateToMs(dateStr) {

  return new Date(dateStr).getTime();

}


function renderChart() {

  const wrap = document.getElementById('chart-wrap');

  let all = [...prevReadings];

  const cd = document.getElementById('rDate').value;

  const crRaw = parseFloat(document.getElementById('creat').value);

  if (cd && crRaw && curEGFR) {

    const scrMgDL = useMgDL ? crRaw : crRaw / 88.42;

    if (!all.find(r => r.date === cd)) {

      all.push({ date: cd, creat_mgdl: scrMgDL, egfr: curEGFR });

      all.sort((a,b) => a.date.localeCompare(b.date));

    }

  }

  if (all.length < 2) { wrap.classList.add('hidden'); return; }

  wrap.classList.remove('hidden');


  // Use real timestamps for proportionate spacing

  const dataPoints = all.map(r => ({ x: dateToMs(r.date), y: r.egfr }));


  // Linear regression on real timestamps

  const n = dataPoints.length;

  const meanX = dataPoints.reduce((s,p)=>s+p.x,0)/n;

  const meanY = dataPoints.reduce((s,p)=>s+p.y,0)/n;

  const slope = dataPoints.reduce((s,p)=>s+(p.x-meanX)*(p.y-meanY),0) /

                dataPoints.reduce((s,p)=>s+(p.x-meanX)**2,0);

  const intercept = meanY - slope * meanX;


  // Project 2 years ahead if we have ≥3 readings

  const projPoints = [];

  if (n >= 3) {

    const lastMs = dataPoints[n-1].x;

    const oneYear = 365.25 * 24 * 3600 * 1000;

    projPoints.push({ x: lastMs, y: dataPoints[n-1].y }); // connect at last real point

    projPoints.push({ x: lastMs + oneYear, y: Math.max(0, Math.round((intercept + slope*(lastMs+oneYear))*10)/10) });

    projPoints.push({ x: lastMs + 2*oneYear, y: Math.max(0, Math.round((intercept + slope*(lastMs+2*oneYear))*10)/10) });

  }


  const ctx = document.getElementById('tChart').getContext('2d');

  if (chartInst) chartInst.destroy();


  const showProj = projPoints.length > 0;


  chartInst = new Chart(ctx, {

    type:'line',

    data:{

      datasets:[

        {

          label:'eGFR',

          data: dataPoints,

          borderColor:'#2c5f8a',

          backgroundColor:'rgba(44,95,138,.07)',

          pointBackgroundColor:'#2c5f8a',

          pointRadius:6,

          pointHoverRadius:8,

          borderWidth:2.5,

          fill:false,

          tension:.3,

        },

        ...(showProj ? [{

          label:'Projected trajectory',

          data: projPoints,

          borderColor:'#c8a84b',

          borderDash:[6,4],

          pointBackgroundColor:'#c8a84b',

          pointRadius:4,

          borderWidth:2,

          fill:false,

          tension:.3,

        }] : [])

      ]

    },

    options:{

      responsive:true,

      plugins:{

        legend:{ display:showProj, position:'top', labels:{font:{family:'DM Sans',size:12},boxWidth:24} },

        tooltip:{

          callbacks:{

            title: items => {

              const d = new Date(items[0].parsed.x);

              return d.toLocaleDateString('en-GB', {day:'numeric',month:'short',year:'numeric'});

            },

            label: c => `${c.dataset.label}: ${c.parsed.y} mL/min/1.73m²`

          }

        }

      },

      scales:{

        x:{

          type:'linear',

          ticks:{

            callback: val => {

              const d = new Date(val);

              return d.toLocaleDateString('en-GB', {month:'short',year:'2-digit'});

            },

            maxRotation:45,

            autoSkip:true,

            maxTicksLimit:8,

          },

          grid:{display:false},

          title:{display:true,text:'Date',font:{family:'DM Sans',size:12}}

        },

        y:{

          min:0,

          max:120,

          title:{display:true,text:'eGFR (mL/min/1.73m²)',font:{family:'DM Sans',size:12}},

          grid:{color:'rgba(0,0,0,.06)'}

        }

      }

    },

    plugins:[{ id:'bands', beforeDraw(ch) {

      const {ctx:cx,chartArea:{left,right},scales:{y}} = ch;

      [[90,120,'rgba(45,122,79,.06)'],[60,90,'rgba(45,122,79,.04)'],[45,60,'rgba(184,134,11,.07)'],[30,45,'rgba(204,85,0,.07)'],[15,30,'rgba(204,85,0,.1)'],[0,15,'rgba(192,57,43,.1)']].forEach(([lo,hi,col])=>{

        const yt=y.getPixelForValue(Math.min(hi,120)), yb=y.getPixelForValue(Math.max(lo,0));

        cx.fillStyle=col; cx.fillRect(left,yt,right-left,yb-yt);

      });

    }}]

  });

}


// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────

// ACR HANDLER

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────

function handleACR(r) {

  document.getElementById('acr-no').classList.add('hidden');

  document.getElementById('acr-yes').classList.add('hidden');

  document.getElementById('kdigo-wrap').classList.add('hidden');

  if (r.value === 'no') document.getElementById('acr-no').classList.remove('hidden');

  else document.getElementById('acr-yes').classList.remove('hidden');

}


function showACR() {

  const rawVal = parseFloat(document.getElementById('acr-in').value);

  const box = document.getElementById('acr-result');

  if (!rawVal || rawVal < 0) { box.innerHTML=''; return; }


  const mgmmol = useACRmgg ? rawVal / 8.84 : rawVal;

  curACR_mgmmol = mgmmol;

  saveToStorage();


  const dispVal = useACRmgg ? rawVal.toFixed(1) + ' mg/g' : rawVal.toFixed(1) + ' mg/mmol';

  let cat, desc, cls;

  if (mgmmol < 3)  { cat='A1 — Normal to mildly increased'; desc='No significant albuminuria.'; cls='green'; }

  else if (mgmmol < 30) { cat='A2 — Moderately increased'; desc='Microalbuminuria detected. An important marker of kidney and cardiovascular risk. Discuss with your GP — an ACE inhibitor or ARB and an SGLT2 inhibitor may be indicated.'; cls='yellow'; }

  else { cat='A3 — Severely increased'; desc='Significant proteinuria — substantially increases CKD progression and cardiovascular risk. GP review and likely nephrology referral warranted. Treatment with an ACE inhibitor or ARB, and an SGLT2 inhibitor, should be discussed.'; cls='orange'; }


  box.innerHTML = `<div class="ib ${cls}"><strong>ACR ${dispVal} — ${cat}</strong><br>${desc}</div>`;


  renderFullStage(curEGFR, mgmmol);

  renderKDIGO(curEGFR, mgmmol);

  renderKFRE(curAge, curSex, curEGFR, mgmmol);

}


// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────

// KDIGO HEATMAP

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────

const KM = [

  [ 1,  2,  3 ], // G1

  [ 1,  2,  3 ], // G2

  [ 2,  3,  4 ], // G3a

  [ 3,  4,  4 ], // G3b

  [ 4,  4,  5 ], // G4

  [ 5,  5,  5 ], // G5

];

const KL = ['Low','Mod. increased','High','Very high','Discuss with GP/specialist'];

const KC = ['hm1','hm2','hm3','hm4','hm5'];


function renderKDIGO(egfr, acrMgMmol) {

  const wrap = document.getElementById('kdigo-wrap');

  wrap.classList.remove('hidden');


  const eIdx = stageOf(egfr).idx;

  const aIdx = acrCatOf(acrMgMmol);


  const eLabels = ['G1 ≥90','G2 60–89','G3a 45–59','G3b 30–44','G4 15–29','G5 &lt;15'];

  const aLabels = ['A1 &lt;3 mg/mmol','A2 3–30 mg/mmol','A3 ≥30 mg/mmol'];


  let t = `<table class="hm-tbl"><thead><tr>

    <th style="text-align:right;padding-right:10px;color:var(--text-muted);font-size:11px">eGFR stage ↓ &nbsp;|&nbsp; ACR category →</th>

    ${aLabels.map((l,ci) => `<th style="${ci===aIdx?'color:var(--accent-dark);font-weight:700;':''}">${l}</th>`).join('')}

  </tr></thead><tbody>`;


  KM.forEach((row, ri) => {

    t += `<tr><td class="hm-row-lbl" style="${ri===eIdx?'color:var(--accent-dark);font-weight:700':''}"><strong>${eLabels[ri]}</strong></td>`;

    row.forEach((risk, ci) => {

      const active = ri===eIdx && ci===aIdx;

      t += `<td class="${KC[risk-1]}${active?' hm-active':''}">${active?'▶ ':''}${KL[risk-1]}</td>`;

    });

    t += `</tr>`;

  });

  t += `</tbody></table>`;

  document.getElementById('hm-container').innerHTML = t;

}


// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────

// KFRE 4-variable (Tangri JASN 2011 / JAMA 2016)

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────

function calcKFRE(age, sex, egfr, acrMgMmol) {

  const female = sex === 'female' ? 1 : 0;

  // Exact 4-variable formula from Tangri lab (kidneyfailurerisk.com R package)

  // Coefficients per Tangri 2011 JASN; S0 values from Tangri 2016 JAMA validation

  // Age is per 10-year increment, centred at 7.036 decades (70.36yr reference)

  const lp = -0.2201 * (age/10 - 7.036)

            + 0.2467 * (female - 0.5)

            - 0.5567 * (Math.log(egfr) - Math.log(29.66))

            + 0.4510 * (Math.log(acrMgMmol) - Math.log(31.67));

  const r2 = 1 - Math.pow(0.9750, Math.exp(lp));

  const r5 = 1 - Math.pow(0.9240, Math.exp(lp));

  return {

    r2: Math.min(99.9, Math.max(0.1, Math.round(r2*1000)/10)),

    r5: Math.min(99.9, Math.max(0.1, Math.round(r5*1000)/10))

  };

}


function renderKFRE(age, sex, egfr, acrMgMmol) {

  const wrap = document.getElementById('kfre-wrap');

  if (!age || !sex || !egfr || !acrMgMmol) { wrap.innerHTML=''; return; }


  // KFRE is only validated for eGFR < 60. Do not display above this threshold.

  if (egfr >= 60) {

    wrap.innerHTML = `

      <div class="sec-lbl">Kidney Failure Risk Estimate (KFRE)</div>

      <div class="ib blue" style="font-size:13px">

        <strong>KFRE not applicable at this eGFR level.</strong> The Kidney Failure Risk Equation (Tangri et al., 2011) was derived and validated in patients with eGFR &lt;60 mL/min/1.73m². Applying it above this threshold produces unreliable estimates and is not recommended. Your current eGFR of ${egfr} mL/min/1.73m² is above the validated range — the KFRE is not shown.

      </div>`;

    return;

  }


  const { r2, r5 } = calcKFRE(age, sex, egfr, acrMgMmol);


  // Pictogram: 10×10 grid, no scrolling needed

  function pictogram(pct, timeframe) {

    const n = Math.round(Math.min(pct, 99));

    const col = pct < 5 ? '#2d7a4f' : pct < 20 ? '#e07020' : '#c0392b';

    const txtCol = pct < 5 ? 'var(--green)' : pct < 20 ? 'var(--orange)' : 'var(--red)';

    const isHighRisk = pct >= 5;

    let sqs = '';

    for (let i = 0; i < 100; i++) {

      sqs += `<div class="psq" style="background:${i < n ? col : '#e2ddd4'}" title="${i < n ? 'At risk' : 'Not at risk'}"></div>`;

    }

    return `

      <div class="kfre-pbox">

        <div style="font-weight:600;font-size:13px;color:var(--text-muted);margin-bottom:4px">${timeframe}</div>

        <div class="kfre-pct" style="color:${txtCol}">${pct}%</div>

        <div style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-muted);margin-bottom:8px">estimated risk of kidney failure</div>

        <div class="pict-wrap">${sqs}</div>

        <div style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text-light);margin-top:6px">Each square = 1 person in 100</div>

        ${isHighRisk ? `<div style="font-size:12px;font-weight:600;color:${col};margin-top:8px;padding:6px 10px;background:${col}22;border-radius:6px;text-align:center">Please discuss these results with your GP or a specialist</div>` : ''}

      </div>`;

  }


  wrap.innerHTML = `

    <div class="sec-lbl">Kidney Failure Risk Estimate (KFRE)</div>

    <div class="ib blue" style="font-size:13px;margin-bottom:16px">

      The <strong>Kidney Failure Risk Equation</strong> (Tangri et al., JASN 2011, validated globally 2016) estimates the probability of needing dialysis or a kidney transplant based on your age, sex, eGFR, and ACR. Each pictogram shows how many people out of 100 with your kidney profile would be expected to reach kidney failure within that time frame.

    </div>

    <div class="kfre-grid">

      ${pictogram(r2, '2-year risk')}

      ${pictogram(r5, '5-year risk')}

    </div>

    <div class="ib gold" style="font-size:13px">

      <strong>Important:</strong> The KFRE is a statistical model based on population data. It tells you what happens <em>on average</em> to people with your profile — not what will happen to you personally. Please discuss this result with your GP or nephrologist alongside your full clinical picture. Do not act on it alone.

    </div>

    <div class="footnote">† The KFRE is validated for eGFR &lt;60 mL/min/1.73m². Results outside this range are not shown.</div>`;

}


// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────

// BLOOD PRESSURE

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────

function handleBP(r) {

  document.getElementById('bp-no').classList.add('hidden');

  document.getElementById('bp-yes').classList.add('hidden');

  if (r.value === 'no') document.getElementById('bp-no').classList.remove('hidden');

  else document.getElementById('bp-yes').classList.remove('hidden');

}

function showBP() {

  const s = parseFloat(document.getElementById('bpS').value);

  const d = parseFloat(document.getElementById('bpD').value);

  const b = document.getElementById('bp-result');

  if (!s || !d) { b.innerHTML=''; return; }


  // Grade each component independently, then take the worse of the two.

  // This means one high value always wins — a normal diastolic never rescues an abnormal systolic.

  function sGrade(v) {

    if (v < 130) return 0;   // optimal

    if (v <= 139) return 1;  // mildly elevated

    if (v <= 159) return 2;  // elevated

    return 3;                // significantly raised

  }

  function dGrade(v) {

    if (v < 80) return 0;

    if (v <= 89) return 1;

    if (v <= 99) return 2;

    return 3;

  }


  const grade = Math.max(sGrade(s), dGrade(d));


  let cls, lbl, adv;

  if (grade === 0) {

    cls='bpg'; lbl='✓ Optimal (&lt; 130/80)';

    adv='Your BP is within the NICE target for CKD (&lt;130/80 mmHg). Continue with a heart-healthy lifestyle and regular monitoring.';

  } else if (grade === 1) {

    cls='bpy'; lbl='⚠ Mildly elevated (130–139/80–89)';

    adv='This level warrants attention in CKD. Lifestyle: reduce salt to &lt;6g/day, maintain a healthy weight, exercise ≥150 min/week, limit alcohol. Recheck monthly. Discuss at your next GP appointment.';

  } else if (grade === 2) {

    cls='bpo'; lbl='⚠ Elevated (140–159/90–99)';

    adv='This BP is above the CKD target of &lt;130/80 mmHg. Please discuss with your GP — medication may be warranted alongside lifestyle measures.';

  } else {

    cls='bpr'; lbl='🔴 Significantly raised (≥ 160 systolic or ≥ 100 diastolic)';

    adv='Please contact your GP or NHS 111 promptly. If you have severe headache, vision changes, chest pain, or breathlessness — call 999 or go to A&amp;E immediately.';

  }

  b.innerHTML = `<div class="bpi ${cls}"><div class="bpdot"></div><div><strong>${s}/${d} mmHg — ${lbl}</strong><br><span style="font-size:13px;margin-top:4px;display:block">${adv}</span></div></div>`;

}


// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────

// PRINT REPORT

// Must be called synchronously from a tap event on mobile

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────

function printReport() {

  if (!curEGFR) { alert('Please calculate your eGFR first before printing.'); return; }

  try {

    buildPrintReport();

  } catch(e) {

    alert('Could not build report: ' + e.message);

    return;

  }

  setTimeout(function() { window.print(); }, 150);

}


function stageColor(egfr) {

  if (egfr >= 60) return 'gn';

  if (egfr >= 45) return 'yl';

  if (egfr >= 15) return 'or';

  return 'rd';

}


function bpGrade(s, d) {

  function sg(v){ return v<130?0:v<=139?1:v<=159?2:3; }

  function dg(v){ return v<80?0:v<=89?1:v<=99?2:3; }

  return Math.max(sg(s),dg(d));

}


function buildPrintReport() {

  const name    = document.getElementById('patientName').value.trim();

  const age     = document.getElementById('age').value;

  const sex     = document.querySelector('input[name="sex"]:checked')?.value || '';

  const rDate   = document.getElementById('rDate').value;

  const creatRaw = parseFloat(document.getElementById('creat').value);

  const scrMgDL = useMgDL ? creatRaw : creatRaw / 88.42;

  const htCm    = getHeightCm();

  const wtKg    = getWeightKg();

  const bmi     = wtKg / ((htCm/100)**2);

  const bpS     = parseFloat(document.getElementById('bpS').value);

  const bpD     = parseFloat(document.getElementById('bpD').value);

  const hasBP   = !isNaN(bpS) && !isNaN(bpD);

  const hasACR  = curACR_mgmmol !== null;


  const si = stageOf(curEGFR);

  const egfrCls = stageColor(curEGFR);


  const fmtD = (ds) => {

    if (!ds) return '—';

    const d = new Date(ds);

    return d.toLocaleDateString('en-GB',{day:'numeric',month:'short',year:'numeric'});

  };


  // Trend data

  let allReadings = [...prevReadings];

  const cd = document.getElementById('rDate').value;

  if (cd && curEGFR && !allReadings.find(r=>r.date===cd)) {

    allReadings.push({date:cd, creat_mgdl:scrMgDL, egfr:curEGFR, cur:true});

    allReadings.sort((a,b)=>a.date.localeCompare(b.date));

  }

  const hasTrend = allReadings.length >= 2;


  // Slope

  let slopePerYear = null;

  if (hasTrend && allReadings.length >= 2) {

    const first = allReadings[0], last = allReadings[allReadings.length-1];

    const years = (new Date(last.date) - new Date(first.date)) / (365.25*24*3600*1000);

    if (years > 0) slopePerYear = (last.egfr - first.egfr) / years;

  }


  // BP label

  let bpLabel = '', bpCls = '';

  if (hasBP) {

    const g = bpGrade(bpS, bpD);

    if (g===0){bpLabel='Optimal (<130/80)';bpCls='gn';}

    else if(g===1){bpLabel='Mildly elevated (130–139/80–89)';bpCls='yl';}

    else if(g===2){bpLabel='Elevated (140–159/90–99)';bpCls='or';}

    else{bpLabel='Significantly raised (≥160/≥100)';bpCls='rd';}

  }


  // ACR label

  let acrLabel='', acrCls='';

  if (hasACR) {

    if (curACR_mgmmol<3){acrLabel='A1 — Normal (<3 mg/mmol)';acrCls='gn';}

    else if(curACR_mgmmol<30){acrLabel='A2 — Moderately increased (3–30 mg/mmol)';acrCls='yl';}

    else{acrLabel='A3 — Severely increased (≥30 mg/mmol)';acrCls='or';}

  }


  // KFRE

  let kfre2='—', kfre5='—', kfrePict2='', kfrePict5='';

  if (hasACR && curEGFR && age && sex) {

    const k = calcKFRE(parseFloat(age), sex, curEGFR, curACR_mgmmol);

    kfre2 = k.r2 + '%'; kfre5 = k.r5 + '%';

    const buildPict = (pct, label) => {

      const n = Math.round(Math.min(pct,99));

      const col = pct<5?'#2d7a4f':pct<20?'#e07020':'#c0392b';

      const txtCol = pct<5?'#2d7a4f':pct<20?'#cc5500':'#c0392b';

      let sq='';

      for(let i=0;i<100;i++) sq+=`<div class="pr-psq" style="background:${i<n?col:'#e2ddd4'}"></div>`;

      return `<div class="pr-pbox">

        <div style="font-size:10px;color:#6b6258;margin-bottom:2px">${label}</div>

        <div class="pr-ppct" style="color:${txtCol}">${pct}%</div>

        <div style="font-size:9px;color:#9a9088;margin-bottom:4px">kidney failure risk</div>

        <div class="pr-pgrid">${sq}</div>

        <div style="font-size:8px;color:#9a9088;margin-top:3px">Each square = 1 in 100</div>

      </div>`;

    };

    kfrePict2 = buildPict(k.r2, '2-year risk');

    kfrePict5 = buildPict(k.r5, '5-year risk');

  }


  // Interpretation boxes — concise for single-page fit

  const interpBoxes = () => {

    let boxes = '';

    // eGFR

    if (curEGFR >= 60) boxes += `<div class="pr-ib gn"><strong>eGFR ${curEGFR} — Stage ${si.stage}.</strong> Mildly reduced or normal. Monitor for ongoing decline.</div>`;

    else if (curEGFR >= 45) boxes += `<div class="pr-ib yl"><strong>eGFR ${curEGFR} — Stage ${si.stage}.</strong> Moderately reduced. Repeat confirmatory test within 8 weeks.</div>`;

    else if (curEGFR >= 30) boxes += `<div class="pr-ib or"><strong>eGFR ${curEGFR} — Stage ${si.stage}.</strong> Moderately–severely reduced. Repeat within 4 weeks. Discuss nephrology referral with GP.</div>`;

    else boxes += `<div class="pr-ib rd"><strong>eGFR ${curEGFR} — Stage ${si.stage}.</strong> Severely reduced. Urgent GP review. Nephrology referral very likely needed.</div>`;


    // Trend

    if (slopePerYear !== null) {

      const absSlope = Math.abs(slopePerYear).toFixed(1);

      if (slopePerYear < -5) boxes += `<div class="pr-ib rd"><strong>Rapid decline: ~${absSlope} mL/min/yr</strong> — above NICE threshold of 5/yr for referral. Discuss urgently with GP.</div>`;

      else if (slopePerYear < -2) boxes += `<div class="pr-ib or"><strong>Progressive decline: ~${absSlope} mL/min/yr.</strong> Review modifiable risk factors (BP, proteinuria, medications).</div>`;

      else if (slopePerYear < 0) boxes += `<div class="pr-ib yl"><strong>Mild decline: ~${absSlope} mL/min/yr.</strong> Within age-related range but warrants monitoring.</div>`;

      else boxes += `<div class="pr-ib gn"><strong>Stable or improving eGFR.</strong> Continue monitoring as advised.</div>`;

    }


    // BP

    if (hasBP) {

      if (bpS < 130 && bpD < 80) boxes += `<div class="pr-ib gn"><strong>BP ${bpS}/${bpD} mmHg — within NICE target (&lt;130/80).</strong> Continue lifestyle and monitoring.</div>`;

      else if (bpGrade(bpS,bpD)===1) boxes += `<div class="pr-ib yl"><strong>BP ${bpS}/${bpD} mmHg — mildly elevated.</strong> Lifestyle measures; discuss at next GP appointment.</div>`;

      else if (bpGrade(bpS,bpD)===2) boxes += `<div class="pr-ib or"><strong>BP ${bpS}/${bpD} mmHg — elevated.</strong> Above the CKD target of &lt;130/80 mmHg. Discuss with your GP — medication may be warranted. An ACE inhibitor or ARB is preferred in CKD with proteinuria; an SGLT2 inhibitor may also be indicated.</div>`;

      else boxes += `<div class="pr-ib rd"><strong>BP ${bpS}/${bpD} mmHg — significantly raised.</strong> Contact your GP or NHS 111 promptly. If you have severe headache, vision changes, chest pain, or breathlessness — call 999 or go to A&E immediately.</div>`;

    }


    // ACR

    if (hasACR) {

      if (curACR_mgmmol < 3) boxes += `<div class="pr-ib gn"><strong>ACR ${curACR_mgmmol.toFixed(1)} mg/mmol — A1, no significant albuminuria.</strong> Continue routine monitoring.</div>`;

      else if (curACR_mgmmol < 30) boxes += `<div class="pr-ib yl"><strong>ACR ${curACR_mgmmol.toFixed(1)} mg/mmol — A2 microalbuminuria.</strong> Raises CKD and CV risk. Treatment with an ACE inhibitor or ARB, and an SGLT2 inhibitor, may be indicated — discuss with GP.</div>`;

      else boxes += `<div class="pr-ib or"><strong>ACR ${curACR_mgmmol.toFixed(1)} mg/mmol — A3 significant proteinuria.</strong> Substantially increases risk. GP review and likely nephrology referral warranted. Treatment with an ACE inhibitor or ARB and an SGLT2 inhibitor should be discussed.</div>`;

    }


    return boxes;

  };


  // Next steps — concise for single-page fit

  const nextSteps = () => {

    const steps = [];

    if (hasBP && bpGrade(bpS,bpD) >= 2) steps.push({urg:true, title:'Discuss BP management with your GP', detail:`${bpS}/${bpD} mmHg exceeds the CKD target of <130/80 mmHg. Medication may be warranted — an ACE inhibitor or ARB is preferred in CKD with proteinuria.`});

    if (hasACR && curACR_mgmmol >= 3) steps.push({urg: curACR_mgmmol >= 30, title:'Ask your GP about ACE inhibitor/ARB and SGLT2 inhibitor', detail: curACR_mgmmol >= 30 ? `ACR ${curACR_mgmmol.toFixed(1)} mg/mmol (A3) — significant proteinuria. NICE NG203 recommends renin-angiotensin system blockade (ACE inhibitor or ARB) and consideration of an SGLT2 inhibitor to reduce progression risk.` : `ACR ${curACR_mgmmol.toFixed(1)} mg/mmol (A2) — microalbuminuria. An ACE inhibitor or ARB and an SGLT2 inhibitor may be indicated to reduce CKD and cardiovascular risk.`});

    if (curEGFR < 30) steps.push({urg:true, title:'Urgent GP review required', detail:`eGFR ${curEGFR} warrants prompt assessment and likely nephrology referral.`});

    else if (curEGFR < 60) steps.push({urg:true, title:`Repeat blood tests within ${curEGFR>=45?'8':'4'} weeks`, detail:'Single readings can be affected by dehydration or illness. Confirmatory result needed before any diagnosis.'});

    else steps.push({urg:false, title:'Repeat blood tests as per GP advice', detail:'Regular monitoring is important to detect trends over time.'});

    if (!hasACR) steps.push({urg:false, title:'Request urine ACR from GP', detail:'First-morning urine sample for albumin — essential for accurate CKD staging.'});

    if (hasTrend && slopePerYear !== null && slopePerYear < -5) steps.push({urg:true, title:'eGFR decline >5/yr — discuss nephrology referral', detail:'NICE NG203 criterion for referral consideration.'});

    steps.push({urg:false, title:'Annual monitoring: eGFR, creatinine, ACR, BP', detail:`NICE NG203: ${si.stage}${hasACR?(curACR_mgmmol<3?' + A1':curACR_mgmmol<30?' + A2':' + A3'):''} warrants at least annual review.`});

    steps.push({urg:false, title:'Lifestyle: salt <6g/day, healthy weight, exercise ≥150 min/week', detail:'Avoid NSAIDs, stay hydrated, inform pharmacist/GP of CKD before new medications.'});

    return steps.map((s,i) => `<div class="pr-step"><div class="pr-stepn${s.urg?' urg':''}">${i+1}</div><div class="pr-stept"><strong>${s.title}</strong><span>${s.detail}</span></div></div>`).join('');

  };


  // KDIGO table

  const kdigoTable = () => {

    if (!hasACR) return '<div style="font-size:11px;color:#9a9088;font-style:italic">ACR not entered — KDIGO risk category unavailable.</div>';

    const eIdx = si.idx;

    const aIdx = acrCatOf(curACR_mgmmol);

    const KM2 = [[1,2,3],[1,2,3],[2,3,4],[3,4,4],[4,4,5],[5,5,5]];

    const KL2 = ['Low','Mod.','High','V.High','Refer'];

    const KC2 = ['pkc1','pkc2','pkc3','pkc4','pkc5'];

    const eL = ['G1 ≥90','G2 60–89','G3a 45–59','G3b 30–44','G4 15–29','G5 <15'];

    const aL = ['A1 <3','A2 3–30','A3 ≥30'];

    let t = `<div class="pr-kdigo">

      <div class="pr-kh"></div>${aL.map((l,ci)=>`<div class="pr-kh" style="${ci===aIdx?'color:#1a3d5c;font-weight:700':''}">${l}</div>`).join('')}`;

    KM2.forEach((row,ri)=>{

      t+=`<div class="pr-kr" style="${ri===eIdx?'color:#1a3d5c;font-weight:700':''}">${eL[ri]}</div>`;

      row.forEach((risk,ci)=>{

        const act=ri===eIdx&&ci===aIdx;

        t+=`<div class="pr-kc ${KC2[risk-1]}${act?' pkc-active':''}">${act?'▶ ':''}${KL2[risk-1]}</div>`;

      });

    });

    t+='</div>';

    return t;

  };


  // Build full report HTML

  const sexLabel = sex ? sex.charAt(0).toUpperCase()+sex.slice(1) : '';

  const creatDisp2 = useMgDL ? creatRaw.toFixed(2)+' mg/dL' : Math.round(creatRaw)+' μmol/L';


  let trendRows = '';

  if (hasTrend) {

    allReadings.forEach(r => {

      const badgeCls = r.egfr>=90?'bg1':r.egfr>=60?'bg2':r.egfr>=45?'bg3a':'bg3b';

      const stage = stageOf(r.egfr).stage;

      trendRows += `<tr${r.cur?' class="cur"':''}>

        <td>${fmtD(r.date)}${r.cur?' ★':''}</td>

        <td>${useMgDL?r.creat_mgdl.toFixed(2)+' mg/dL':Math.round(r.creat_mgdl*88.42)+' μmol/L'}</td>

        <td>${r.egfr}</td>

        <td><span class="pr-badge ${badgeCls}">${stage}</span></td>

      </tr>`;

    });

    if (slopePerYear !== null) {

      const last = allReadings[allReadings.length-1];

      const proj5 = Math.max(0,(last.egfr + slopePerYear*5).toFixed(1));

      const proj10 = Math.max(0,(last.egfr + slopePerYear*10).toFixed(1));

      if (slopePerYear < 0) {

        trendRows += `<tr class="proj"><td>~5 yrs (projected)</td><td>—</td><td>~${proj5}</td><td><span class="pr-badge ${proj5>=60?'bg2':proj5>=45?'bg3a':'bg3b'}">${stageOf(parseFloat(proj5)).stage}</span></td></tr>`;

        trendRows += `<tr class="proj"><td>~10 yrs (projected)</td><td>—</td><td>~${proj10}</td><td><span class="pr-badge ${proj10>=60?'bg2':proj10>=45?'bg3a':'bg3b'}">${stageOf(parseFloat(proj10)).stage}</span></td></tr>`;

      }

    }

  }


  const html = `

  <div class="pr-hdr">

    <div class="pr-logo">

      <img function buildKfrePict(pct, label) {

  const n = Math.round(Math.min(pct,99));

  const col = pct<5?'#2d7a4f':pct<20?'#e07020':'#c0392b';

  const txtCol = pct<5?'#2d7a4f':pct<20?'#cc5500':'#c0392b';

  let sq='';

  for(let i=0;i<100;i++) sq+=`<div class="pr-psq" style="background:${i<n?col:'#e2ddd4'}"></div>`;

  return `<div class="pr-pbox">

    <div style="font-size:10px;color:#6b6258;margin-bottom:2px">${label}</div>

    <div class="pr-ppct" style="color:${txtCol}">${pct}%</div>

    <div style="font-size:9px;color:#9a9088;margin-bottom:4px">kidney failure risk</div>

    <div class="pr-pgrid">${sq}</div>

    <div style="font-size:8px;color:#9a9088;margin-top:3px">Each square = 1 in 100</div>

  </div>`;

}


// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────

// RESET — clear localStorage and wipe the form

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────

function resetData() {

  if (!confirm('Clear all saved data and start over?')) return;


  // Clear storage

  try { localStorage.removeItem(LS_KEY); } catch(e) {}


  // Reset all state variables

  useMgDL = false;

  useACRmgg = false;

  useImperialHeight = false;

  useImperialWeight = false;

  curEGFR = null; curAge = null; curSex = null;

  curACR_mgmmol = null;

  prevReadings = [];

  if (chartInst) { chartInst.destroy(); chartInst = null; }


  // Reset all form inputs

  document.getElementById('patientName').value = '';

  document.getElementById('age').value = '';

  document.getElementById('creat').value = '';

  document.getElementById('height').value = '';

  document.getElementById('htFt').value = '';

  document.getElementById('htIn').value = '';

  document.getElementById('weight').value = '';

  document.getElementById('wtSt').value = '';

  document.getElementById('wtLbs').value = '';

  document.getElementById('bpS').value = '';

  document.getElementById('bpD').value = '';

  document.getElementById('acr-in').value = '';

  document.getElementById('prev-date').value = '';

  document.getElementById('prev-creat').value = '';

  document.getElementById('rDate').value = new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0];


  // Reset radio buttons

  document.getElementById('sM').checked = true;

  document.querySelectorAll('input[name="fr"]').forEach(r => r.checked = false);

  document.querySelectorAll('input[name="acr"]').forEach(r => r.checked = false);

  document.querySelectorAll('input[name="bp"]').forEach(r => r.checked = false);


  // Reset unit toggles to defaults

  document.getElementById('creatToggle').checked = false; toggleCreat();

  document.getElementById('htToggle').checked = false; toggleHeight();

  document.getElementById('wtToggle').checked = false; toggleWeight();

  document.getElementById('acrToggle').checked = false;


  // Hide all result cards

  ['c-results','c-trend','c-acr','c-bp','c-report','c-res'].forEach(id =>

    document.getElementById(id).classList.add('hidden'));


  // Hide all sub-sections

  ['fr-advice','multi-readings','acr-no','acr-yes','kdigo-wrap',

   'chart-wrap','bp-no','bp-yes','acr-result','cg-section'].forEach(id => {

    const el = document.getElementById(id);

    if (el) el.classList.add('hidden');

  });


  // Clear dynamic content

  ['advice-boxes','r-list','retest-box','acr-result','bp-result',

   'hm-container','kfre-wrap','egfr-val','ckd-stage','ckd-desc','ckd-full-stage','bmi-val','bmi-flag','cg-val'].forEach(id => {

    const el = document.getElementById(id);

    if (el) el.innerHTML = el.id === 'egfr-val' ? '—' : el.id === 'ckd-stage' ? '—' : el.id === 'ckd-desc' ? '—' : el.id === 'bmi-val' ? '—' : el.id === 'cg-val' ? '—' : '';

  });


  // Scroll back to top

  window.scrollTo({ top: 0, behavior: 'smooth' });

}


// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────

// LIVE RECALC — called on any input change once results are showing

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────

function liveRecalc() {

  // Only recalc if results are already visible (i.e. user has already hit Calculate once)

  if (document.getElementById('c-results').classList.contains('hidden')) return;

  // Silent recalc — no alert, no scroll

  calculate(true);

  // Cascade: re-render ACR if it's already been entered

  const acrVal = parseFloat(document.getElementById('acr-in').value);

  if (curACR_mgmmol !== null && acrVal) { showACR(); }

  // Cascade: re-render BP if already entered

  const bpS = document.getElementById('bpS').value;

  const bpD = document.getElementById('bpD').value;

  if (bpS && bpD) { showBP(); }

  // Cascade: re-render chart/list if trend section is open

  const multiOpen = !document.getElementById('multi-readings').classList.contains('hidden');

  if (multiOpen) { renderList(); renderChart(); }

  // Cascade: re-render retest box if single-reading section is open

  const retestOpen = !document.getElementById('fr-advice').classList.contains('hidden');

  if (retestOpen) { renderRetest(curEGFR); }

  // Save updated state

  saveToStorage();

}


// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────

// INIT — restore saved data on load, wire live listeners

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────

window.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {

  // Set today's date as default

  const today = new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0];

  if (!document.getElementById('rDate').value) {

    document.getElementById('rDate').value = today;

  }

  loadFromStorage();


  // Wire every primary input to liveRecalc

  // Main inputs

  ['age','height','weight','htFt','htIn','wtSt','wtLbs','creat','rDate'].forEach(id => {

    const el = document.getElementById(id);

    if (el) {

      el.addEventListener('input', liveRecalc);

      el.addEventListener('change', liveRecalc);

    }

  });

  // Sex radio buttons

  document.querySelectorAll('input[name="sex"]').forEach(r =>

    r.addEventListener('change', liveRecalc)

  );

  // ACR input — already has oninput=showACR but showACR also needs recalc trigger

  // We hook it so showACR updates curACR_mgmmol then liveRecalc re-renders KDIGO/KFRE

  const acrIn = document.getElementById('acr-in');

  if (acrIn) acrIn.addEventListener('input', () => { showACR(); });


  // BP inputs already have oninput=showBP — that's fine, no recalc needed for BP standalone

  // But we need liveRecalc when BP changes so the print report updates

  ['bpS','bpD'].forEach(id => {

    const el = document.getElementById(id);

    if (el) el.addEventListener('input', () => { showBP(); saveToStorage(); });

  });

});

</script>

</body>

</html>
